    			Nb
    			=
    			Nf*Nc
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			x_cell
    			=
    			L/Nc
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			x_sin
    			=
    			x_cell/Nf
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			A_sin
    			=
    			pi*y_sin^2
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			A_dis
    			=
    			pi*(y_sin+y_dis)^2-A_sin
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			A_sindis
    			=
    			2*pi*y_sin*x_sin
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			Vol_sin
    			=
    			A_sin*x_sin
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			Vol_dis
    			=
    			A_dis*x_sin
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			Vol_cell
    			=
    			pi*(y_sin+y_dis+y_cell)^2*x_cell-pi*(y_sin+y_dis)^2*x_cell
    			
					
    						
    
		    		
    
    			Vol_pp
    			=
    			Vol_sin
